 jab bas gless nadi paar kar rahi thi tabhi yah haadasa ho gaya

 tippaniyan The statement of the President's office said that nine people have either been saved or they have managed to escape by swimming on their own
 durghatana somvaar ko haiti ke dakshini praaia:dweep main sthit pastel shahar ke paas hui
 Mari Alta jean-baptiste, director of Haiti's public security office, said the bus driver seems to have ignored warnings not to cross the river
 raashtrapati karyaalay ke bayaan main kaha gaya he ki nau logon ko yaa to bachaa liya gaya he yaa phir vah khud hi tair kar bachane main safal rahe
 The accident occurred on Monday near the town of Pestel, located in the southernmost island of Haiti
 haiti ke jansuraksha karyaalay kii nideshak maari alta jyaan-baptist ne kaha ki aisa lagata he ki bas chaalak ne nadi paar na karne kii chetavaniyon ko nazarandaaj kiya

 Soon the next generation smartphones will be available in the market at very cheap prices
 inaki khaasiyat hogi ki ye aadhuniktam 4ji technology se las honge

 jaldi hi agle jenereshan ke smartphone behad saste daamon main bazaar main uplabdh honge

 inaki keemat behad kam yani 100 dollar (6200 rupee) hogi
 In the next year and a half, such phones will start being received
 mobile phone ke chips banane vaali company broadcom ne yah jaankaree di
 Company's senior director Michael Civello said that operators in the US are ready to buy 4G mobile phones for $ 100
 abhi turant aisa nahin ho paaya he lekin 18 maheenon main yah sambhav ho jayega
 4G technology is five times faster than its predecessor 3G but the handsets running on it are expensive now
 bharat main 4ji se chalane vaala handset kam se kam 18,000 rupee kaa he lekin adhiktar handset 40,000 rupee se kam nahin hai
 In contrast, 3g-equipped phones have become cheaper and their prices have come down to Rs 4,000
 >civilo ne kaha ki bharat main isaki keemten isaki bikri ke wolum par or reliance jeeyo infocom par nirbhar karegi jiske paas desh bhar main 4ji spectrum kaa theka he
 Prices will depend on these only
 duusari baat yah hogi ki parmaanu hathiyaar mukt deshon ke alaava duusare desh siese par hastakshar nahin karne kaa rasta apanaayenge

 china kaa suzav he ki enesji ko aage vichaar vimarsh kar aisa rasta nikaalnaa chahie jo sabhi pakshon ko sweekaar ho or parmaanu aprasar vyavastha bhi bani rahe

 The solution will depend on the extent to which the ruling party and the opposition are able to come together within the Parliament and Anna Hazare will sit on a fast in Mumbai for these three days
 duusari ore, bhaajapa or vam dalon ne sanshodhan pesh karne ke liye notice diya he
 He has decided to introduce some amendments to the Lokpal and Lokayukta Bill, 2011
 anna hajaare ne apane gaanv ralegan siddhi se sadak maarg se chah ghante kaa mumbai kaa safar kiya or ab vah mumbai ke mrdie maidan main anshan par baithenge
 The government has asked Team Anna to wait for the Parliament's decision on the bill, but Hazare hinted that there would be no softening in his stand a day before he sat on a fast at the MMRDA ground in Mumbai
 Compromise is not possible
 viral sankraman se jujh rahe 74 varshiya hajaare ne sehat durust nahin hone ke bich bhi kaha ki vah apana anshan karenge or unhone yah daawa bhi kiya ki unka andolan kisi vyakti, paksh yaa dal ke khilaaf nahin he

 But the question is "what will happen to you"? kaledhan ko waapas laane ke mudde par baba ramdev dwaara rashtriya rajdhani sthit ramlila maidan main anshan shuru kiye jane ke saath hi yogasana or bhajanon kaa daur bhi shuru ho gaya he
 Hundreds of people are queuing up outside the venue of the fast
 ramdev apane samarthakon kii taaliyon kii gadgadaahat ke bich subah kareeb 4 bajkar 50 minute par manchasin hue
 He taught Yogasan to the supporters between 5 am and 7 am
 yogaguru apane anshan ke saath hi ramlila maidan par ashtaang yoga shivi bhi chalaa rahe hai
 He started his fast at 7 in the morning and with this, slogans like Bharat Mata ki jai and corruption will be eradicated, will save the country
 subah 7 baje ke baad se hi ramlila maidan par bhajan gane kaa silsilaa bhi chal rahaa he
 All musical instruments are also present on the stage to sing bhajans
 ramdev apane kareebi logon ke saath 12 foot kii oonchai par banaae gaye 1,200 vargafoot ke manch par baithe hai
 There is a queue of about one kilometer long outside the Ramlila grounds and people are eagerly waiting to get inside the grounds
 haalanki, pravesh karne se pehle ramdev ke samarthakon ko kadi suraksha jaanch se guzarana pad rahaa he
 The Delhi Police has made tight security arrangements at the Ramlila Maidan in view of the large gathering of people in large numbers
 dilli police ke pulicekarmiyon ke saath hi commando bhi morcha sanbhale hue hai
